### [48] [Identity-Consistent Multi-Pose Generation of Contactless Fingerprints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03830)
*Zhiyu Pan,Xiongjun Guan,Jianjiang Feng,Jie Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 IMPOSE，通过身份一致的多姿态非接触指纹合成数据增强跨模态指纹识别，并在 UWA 与 PolyU CL2CB 数据库上显著降低 EER。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非接触指纹采集更卫生、灵活，但自由手指姿态会带来严重非线性几何畸变，导致其与传统接触式指纹之间存在明显跨模态域差异；现有几何校正或增强方法在极端姿态下鲁棒性不足。

Method: IMPOSE 包含三阶段：首先用带离散码本表示的潜在扩散模型生成滚动指纹身份；其次以 Sauvola 局部自适应二值化作为身份锚点，将滚动指纹翻译为非接触模态；最后通过 3D 手指模型纹理映射与投影进行物理启发的多姿态仿真，生成保持脊线拓扑身份一致且与标准指纹坐标空间对齐的样本。

Result: 在 UWA 和 PolyU CL2CB 上，用 IMPOSE 合成数据微调固定长度密集描述子 FDD 后达到跨模态匹配 SOTA，EER 分别降至 8.74% 与 2.26%；对 DeepPrint、AFRNet 等主流表示也带来稳定收益，合成数据与真实数据结合效果最佳。

Conclusion: IMPOSE 表明，物理启发且身份一致的多姿态合成数据能有效缓解接触式与非接触式指纹识别的跨模态差异，提升多种指纹表示的匹配性能，尤其适用于真实多姿态数据不足的场景。

Abstract: Contactless fingerprint recognition has gained increasing attention due to its advantages in hygiene and acquisition flexibility. However, the absence of physical contact constraints introduces severe nonlinear geometric distortions caused by free finger poses in 3D space, resulting in a substantial cross-modal domain gap between contactless and conventional contact-based fingerprints. Existing solutions largely rely on explicit geometric correction or image enhancement, which are fragile under extreme pose variations. In this paper, we propose Identity-Consistent Multi-Pose Generation of Contactless Fingerprints (IMPOSE), a physics-inspired framework that synthesizes identity-preserving, multi-pose contactless fingerprint samples to empower recognition models. IMPOSE consists of three stages: (1) rolled fingerprint identity generation via latent diffusion with discrete codebook representations, (2) cross-modal translation from rolled to contactless modality guided by Sauvola-based local adaptive binarization as an identity anchor, and (3) physics-based multi-pose simulation through 3D finger model texture mapping and projection. The generated samples maintain strict identity consistency at the ridge topology level and spatial alignment with standard fingerprint coordinate space. Extensive experiments on the UWA and PolyU CL2CB databases demonstrate that fine-tuning fixed-length dense descriptors (FDD) with IMPOSE-synthesized data achieves state-of-the-art cross-modal matching, reducing EER to 8.74% on UWA and 2.26% on PolyU CL2CB. Synthetic data also yields consistent gains across mainstream representations including DeepPrint and AFRNet, and the hybrid strategy combining synthetic and real data achieves the best overall results. The code and generated samples are available at https://github.com/Yu-Yy/IMPOSE.

### [49] [Conditions for well-posed color recovery in scattering media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03837)
*Grigory Solomatov,Derya Akkaynak*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究散射介质中图像场景颜色恢复的适定性条件，指出仅提升传感器无法消除介质参数未知带来的歧义，并提出利用跨像素恢复模式约束解空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 散射介质中的颜色恢复是光学成像中的基础逆问题，但由于光谱信号投影到像素强度以及介质参数未知，同一观测可能对应多个真实颜色解，导致问题本质上病态且误差难以控制。

Method: 作者从成像物理模型出发分析病态性的来源，提出使散射介质中颜色恢复变为适定的充分条件；进一步定义图像中自然出现的跨像素关系，即恢复模式，并在理想高光谱相机条件下证明这些关系可将候选解限制为唯一解。

Result: 研究表明，单纯改进传感器并不足以解决介质诱导的颜色失真；在引入合适的跨像素约束后，理想高光谱观测下的颜色恢复可以获得唯一候选解。

Conclusion: 该工作为散射环境中的定量视觉分析提供了第一性原理基础，表明通过结合物理模型与图像内在跨像素结构，可以构建更可靠的新型颜色恢复算法。

Abstract: Recovering scene color from images captured in scattering media is a fundamental inverse problem in optical imaging. Yet the problem is intrinsically ill-posed as multiple solutions can explain the same observation, and prediction error cannot be controlled without understanding the space of candidate solutions. Here, we present sufficient conditions under which color recovery in a scattering medium becomes well-posed. Observing that ill-posedness stems from (i) projection of spectral signals onto pixel intensities, and (ii) unknown medium parameters, we demonstrate that sensor improvements alone cannot resolve medium-induced distortions without additional constraints. We identify recovery patterns, cross-pixel relationships that naturally occur in images, and prove, for an ideal hyperspectral camera, that they restrict the solution to a unique candidate. This opens the door to a new class of vision algorithms grounded in first principles, enabling quantitative analysis of images in scattering environments.

</details>


### [50] [Parameter-Efficient Multi-View Proficiency Estimation: From Discriminative Classification to Generative Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03848)
*Edoardo Bianchi,Antonio Liotta*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动作熟练度估计关注“动作做得多好”而非“做了什么动作”，对指导训练、康复评估和人才识别很重要；难点在于熟练度差异往往体现在细微的时序、平衡、身体机制和执行质量上，并可能分散在多视角和短时关键片段中。

Method: SkillFormer 采用参数高效的判别式架构进行选择性多视角融合；PATS 通过保留局部密集的基础动作片段改进时间采样；ProfVLM 将熟练度估计转化为条件语言生成任务，利用门控跨视角投影器和紧凑语言骨干同时输出熟练度标签与专家式反馈。

Result: 这些方法在 Ego-Exo4D 上达到当前最优准确率，相比视频 Transformer 基线最多减少 20 倍可训练参数，并最多减少 3 倍训练轮次，同时从封闭集分类推进到可解释反馈生成。

Conclusion: 该方向正从单纯分类转向高效、多视角、可解释的系统设计，核心趋势是结合选择性视角融合、熟练度感知采样和可操作的生成式反馈。

Abstract: Estimating how well a person performs an action, rather than which action is performed, is central to coaching, rehabilitation, and talent identification. This task is challenging because proficiency is encoded in subtle differences in timing, balance, body mechanics, and execution, often distributed across multiple views and short temporal events. We discuss three recent contributions to multi-view proficiency estimation on Ego-Exo4D. SkillFormer introduces a parameter-efficient discriminative architecture for selective multi-view fusion; PATS improves temporal sampling by preserving locally dense excerpts of fundamental movements; and ProfVLM reformulates proficiency estimation as conditional language generation, producing both a proficiency label and expert-style feedback through a gated cross-view projector and a compact language backbone. Together, these methods achieve state-of-the-art accuracy on Ego-Exo4D with up to 20x fewer trainable parameters and up to 3x fewer training epochs than video-transformer baselines, while moving from closed-set classification toward interpretable feedback generation. These results highlight a shift toward efficient, multi-view systems that combine selective fusion, proficiency-aware sampling, and actionable generative feedback.

### [51] [Stream-R1: Reliability-Perplexity Aware Reward Distillation for Streaming Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03849)
*Bin Wu,Mengqi Huang,Shaojin Wu,Weinan Jia,Yuxin Wang,Zhendong Mao,Yongdong Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 Stream-R1，用奖励模型同时衡量蒸馏监督在 rollout 层面的可靠性与帧/空间区域层面的优化价值，从而自适应重加权 DMD 目标，提升自回归流式视频扩散模型的蒸馏质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 DMD 的加速蒸馏方法通常对所有学生 rollout、视频帧和像素赋予相同权重，忽略了不同 rollout 监督信号可靠性不同，以及不同空间区域和时间帧对质量改进贡献不同的问题，导致蒸馏质量受限。

Method: 提出 Reliability-Perplexity Aware Reward Distillation 框架 Stream-R1。其在 Inter-Reliability 层面使用预训练视频奖励分数的指数形式缩放每个 rollout 的损失，使更可靠的监督占主导；在 Intra-Perplexity 层面通过同一奖励模型反向传播得到逐像素梯度显著性，并分解为空间权重与时间权重，将优化集中在更有改进潜力的区域和帧上。同时引入自适应平衡机制，避免视觉质量、运动质量和文本对齐任一维度主导训练。

Result: 在标准流式视频生成基准上，Stream-R1 相比蒸馏基线在视觉质量、运动质量和文本对齐三个维度均取得一致提升。

Conclusion: Stream-R1 通过统一的奖励引导重加权机制更精细地利用蒸馏监督，在不改变模型架构且不增加推理成本的情况下提升流式视频扩散模型的蒸馏性能。

Abstract: Distillation-based acceleration has become foundational for making autoregressive streaming video diffusion models practical, with distribution matching distillation (DMD) as the de facto choice. Existing methods, however, train the student to match the teacher's output indiscriminately, treating every rollout, frame, and pixel as equally reliable supervision. We argue that this caps distilled quality, since it overlooks two complementary axes of variance in DMD supervision: Inter-Reliability across student rollouts whose supervision varies in reliability, and Intra-Perplexity across spatial regions and temporal frames that contribute unequally to where quality can still be improved. The objective thus conflates two questions under a uniform weight: whether to learn from each rollout, and where to concentrate optimization within it. To address this, we propose Stream-R1, a Reliability-Perplexity Aware Reward Distillation framework that adaptively reweights the distillation objective at both rollout and spatiotemporal-element levels through a single shared reward-guided mechanism. At the Inter-Reliability level, Stream-R1 rescales each rollout's loss by an exponential of a pretrained video reward score, so that rollouts with reliable supervision dominate optimization. At the Intra-Perplexity level, it back-propagates the same reward model to extract per-pixel gradient saliency, which is factored into spatial and temporal weights that concentrate optimization pressure on regions and frames where refinement yields the largest expected gain. An adaptive balancing mechanism prevents any single quality axis from dominating across visual quality, motion quality, and text alignment. Stream-R1 attains consistent improvements on all three dimensions over distillation baselines on standard streaming video generation benchmarks, without architectural modification or additional inference cost.

</details>


### [52] [A Deeper Dive into the Irreversibility of PolyProtect: Making Protected Face Templates Harder to Invert](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03857)
*Vedrana Krivokuća Hahn,Jérémy Maceiras,Sébastien Marcel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文重新评估 PolyProtect 生物特征模板保护方法的不可逆性，指出基于余弦距离的数值求解比欧氏距离更容易反演模板，并提出密钥选择算法以提升反演难度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PolyProtect 通过多元多项式将人脸嵌入转换为受保护模板，但其“不可逆性”安全属性需要更深入验证；同时，不同重叠参数下存在不可逆性与识别准确率的权衡，需要更可控的机制。

Method: 作者先比较使用余弦距离与欧氏距离的数值反演求解器，证明余弦距离更有效；随后提出密钥选择算法，为每个主体选择多项式系数和指数，使生成模板更难反演；并研究嵌入值域及归一化对 PolyProtected 域识别准确率的影响。

Result: 实验表明，余弦距离反演比早期工作中的欧氏距离更容易成功；所提出的密钥选择算法能显著提高模板反演难度，并近似均衡不同重叠参数下的不可逆性；嵌入归一化可改善 PolyProtected 域中的识别准确率。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了 PolyProtect 在不可逆性评估中的潜在弱点，并通过密钥选择与嵌入归一化提升了安全性和实用性，使不可逆性与准确率之间的权衡更易控制。

Abstract: This work presents a deeper analysis of the "irreversibility" property of PolyProtect, a biometric template protection method initially proposed for securing face embeddings. PolyProtect transforms embeddings into protected templates via multivariate polynomials, whose coefficients and exponents are distinct for each subject enrolled in the face recognition system. A polynomial is applied to consecutive sets of elements from a given embedding, where the amount of overlap between the sets is a tunable parameter. We begin our irreversibility analysis by demonstrating that PolyProtected templates are easier to invert using a numerical solver based on cosine distance, as opposed to Euclidean distance (used in the earlier PolyProtect work). To make this inversion more difficult, we then propose a "key selection algorithm", which tries to choose "keys" (coefficients and exponents of the PolyProtect polynomial) that enhance the irreversibility of PolyProtected templates, compared to when the keys are purely random. Our experiments show that this algorithm is effective at generating PolyProtected templates that are significantly more difficult to invert, and that it approximately equalises the irreversibility of PolyProtected templates generated using different "overlap" parameters. This allows for better control of the irreversibility versus accuracy trade-off, known to exist across different overlaps. We also show that accuracy in the PolyProtected domain can be affected by the range in which the embedding elements lie, but that this can be improved by normalizing the embeddings prior to applying PolyProtect. This work is reproducible using our open-source code.

### [53] [DMGD: Train-Free Dataset Distillation with Semantic-Distribution Matching in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03877)
*Qichao Wang,Yunhong Lu,Hengyuan Cao,Junyi Zhang,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散模型的数据集蒸馏方法通常依赖额外微调阶段，训练成本较高；同时，有效的生成引导机制尚未充分探索，导致合成数据在语义一致性、多样性和目标分布对齐方面仍有提升空间。

Method: 提出 Dual Matching Guided Diffusion（DMGD）框架，核心是训练无关的高效引导。方法包括：通过条件似然优化建立 Semantic Matching，避免使用辅助分类器；设计动态引导机制，在保持语义对齐的同时提升合成数据多样性；引入基于最优传输的 Distribution Matching，使合成数据分布更贴近目标数据结构；进一步提出 Distribution Approximate Matching 与 Greedy Progressive Matching 以降低分布匹配的计算开销。

Result: 在 ImageNet-Woof、ImageNet-Nette 和 ImageNet-1K 上，DMGD 相比需要额外微调的 SOTA 方法分别取得平均 2.1%、5.4% 和 2.4% 的准确率提升。

Conclusion: DMGD 证明了无需微调的扩散式数据集蒸馏可以通过双重匹配引导实现高效且高质量的合成数据生成，在性能和计算效率上均具有优势。

Abstract: Dataset distillation enables efficient training by distilling the information of large-scale datasets into significantly smaller synthetic datasets. Diffusion based paradigms have emerged in recent years, offering novel perspectives for dataset distillation. However, they typically necessitate additional fine-tuning stages, and effective guidance mechanisms remain underexplored. To address these limitations, we rethink diffusion based dataset distillation and propose a Dual Matching Guided Diffusion (DMGD) framework, centered on efficient training-free guidance. We first establish Semantic Matching via conditional likelihood optimization, eliminating the need for auxiliary classifiers. Furthermore, we propose a dynamic guidance mechanism that enhances the diversity of synthetic data while maintaining semantic alignment. Simultaneously, we introduce an optimal transport (OT) based Distribution Matching approach to further align with the target distribution structure. To ensure efficiency, we develop two enhanced strategies for diffusion based framework: Distribution Approximate Matching and Greedy Progressive Matching. These strategies enable effective distribution matching guidance with minimal computational overhead. Experimental results on ImageNet-Woof, ImageNet-Nette, and ImageNet-1K demonstrate that our training-free approach achieves significant improvements, outperforming state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods requiring additional fine-tuning by average accuracy gains of 2.1%, 5.4%, and 2.4%, respectively.

### [54] [Raising the Ceiling: Better Empirical Fixation Densities for Saliency Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03885)
*Susmit Agrawal,Jannis Hollman,Matthias Kümmerer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出传统固定带宽各向同性高斯 KDE 对人眼注视密度的估计已不适合当前逐图像、样本级显著性评估需求，提出一种逐图像优化的混合密度模型，显著提高了观察者间一致性估计，并揭示现有显著性模型仍有改进空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经验注视密度是显著性模型基准评测的核心，会影响排行榜、失败案例分析和关于人类视觉行为的科学结论。然而长期使用的固定带宽高斯 KDE 方法过于简单，尤其在逐图像评估、逆向基准测试和失败案例分析中可能导致不可靠的密度估计。

Method: 作者提出一个原则化混合模型：结合基于 Abramson 方法的自适应带宽 KDE、中心偏置成分、均匀分布成分以及先进显著性模型成分，用于刻画不同空间与语义来源的观察者一致性；所有参数通过留一被试交叉验证在每张图像上单独优化。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上，该方法得到更高的观察者间一致性估计；每张图像的中位 log-likelihood 提升约 5–15%，AUC 最高提升约 2 个百分点；受影响最大的图像提升超过 25%。

Conclusion: 经验注视密度不应被视为固定不变的真实标签，而应视为可随估计方法改进而演化的统计估计。更准确的注视密度有助于更可靠地评估显著性模型并发现其剩余失败模式。

Abstract: Empirical fixation densities, spatial distributions estimated from human eye-tracking data, are foundational to saliency benchmarking. They directly shape benchmark conclusions, leaderboard rankings, failure case analyses, and scientific claims about human visual behavior. Yet the standard estimation method, fixed-bandwidth isotropic Gaussian KDE, has gone essentially unchanged for decades. This matters now more than ever: as the field shifts toward sample-level evaluation (failure case analysis, inverse benchmarking, per-image model comparison), reliable per-image density estimates become critical. We propose a principled mixture model that combines an adaptive-bandwidth KDE based on Abramson's method, center bias and uniform components, and a state-of-the-art saliency model, to capture different spatial and semantic types of interobserver consistency, and optimize all parameters per image via leave-one-subject-out cross-validation. Our method yields substantially higher interobserver consistency estimates across multiple benchmarks, with median per-image gains of 5-15% in log-likelihood and up to 2 percentage points in AUC. For the most affected images -- precisely those most relevant to failure case analysis -- improvements exceed 25%. We leverage these improved estimates to identify and analyze remaining failure cases of state-of-the-art saliency models, demonstrating that significant headroom for model improvement remains. More broadly, our findings highlight that empirical fixation densities should not be treated as fixed ground truths but as evolving estimates that improve with better methodology.

*Xiaowen Sun,Matthias Kerzel,Mengdi Li,Xufeng Zhao,Paul Striker,Stefan Wermter*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者将数值推理视为视觉语言模型中的回归问题，提出辅助回归损失 ARL：在微调阶段利用 box decoder 输出计算回归损失，同时在推理阶段仍保持标准序列预测形式。基于该策略训练 StateVLM，使模型学习细粒度物体表征，包括目标位置、物体状态位置和可抓取区域。同时构建开源 OSAR 基准，包含 1,172 个场景、7,746 个物体及其边界框标注。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown remarkable performance in various robotic tasks, as they can perceive visual information and understand natural language instructions. However, when applied to robotics, VLMs remain subject to a fundamental limitation inherent in large language models (LLMs): they struggle with numerical reasoning, particularly in object detection and object-state localization. To explore numerical reasoning as a regression task in VLMs, we propose a novel training strategy to adapt VLMs for object detection and object-state localization. This approach leverages box decoder outputs to compute an Auxiliary Regression Loss (ARL) during fine-tuning, while preserving standard sequence prediction at inference. We leverage this training strategy to develop StateVLM (State-aware Vision-Language Model), a novel model designed to perceive and learn fine-grained object representations, including precise localization of objects and their states, as well as graspable regions. Experiments on the OSAR benchmark further support this finding, showing that StateVLM with ARL achieves an average of 5.2\% higher performance than models without ARL. ### [58] [UnAC: Adaptive Visual Prompting with Abstraction and Stepwise Checking for Complex Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03950)
*Yifan Wang,Yun Fu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出 UnAC（Understanding, Abstracting, and Checking）多模态提示方法，通过自适应视觉提示、图像抽象与逐步自检提升大语言多模态模型在复杂视觉推理任务中的可靠性。

Abstract: Although recent LMMs have become much stronger at visual perception, they remain unreliable on problems that require multi-step reasoning over visual evidence. To improve image understanding and capture fine details, we propose an adaptive visual prompting strategy that enables LMMs to focus on salient regions. We further design an image-abstraction prompt to effectively extract key information from images. In addition, we introduce a gradual self-checking scheme that improves reasoning by verifying each decomposed subquestion and its answer. Extensive experiments on three public benchmarks-MathVista, MM-Vet, and MMMU.

### [61] [Large-Scale High-Quality 3D Gaussian Head Reconstruction from Multi-View Captures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04035)
*Evangelos Ntavelis,Sean Wu,Mohamad Shahbazi,Fabio Maninchedda,Dmitry Kostiaev,Artem Sevastopolsky,Vittorio Megaro,Trevor Phillips,Alejandro Blumentals,Shridhar Ravikumar,Mehak Gupta,Reinhard Knothe,Jeronimo Bayer,Matthias Vestner,Simon Schaefer,Thomas Etterlin,Christian Zimmermann,Mathias Deschler,Peter Kaufmann,Stefan Brugger,Sebastian Martin,Brian Amberg,Tom Runia*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HeadsUp 是一种可扩展的前馈式多视图 3D Gaussian 头部重建方法，可在无需测试时优化的情况下为新身份生成高质量三维头部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多视图人头重建方法往往受限于输入视图数量、图像分辨率、模型容量或测试时优化成本，难以利用大规模高分辨率多相机数据实现高质量且可泛化的重建。

Method: 方法采用高效的编码器—解码器架构，将多视图输入压缩为紧凑潜变量，再解码为锚定在中性头部模板上的 UV 参数化 3D Gaussians；该表示使 Gaussian 数量与输入图像数量和分辨率解耦，从而支持大量高分辨率视图训练。

Result: 在超过 10,000 名受试者的内部数据集上训练和评估，HeadsUp 达到当前最优重建质量，并能泛化到新身份，无需测试时优化；论文还分析了身份数量、视图数量和模型容量对性能的缩放规律。

Conclusion: HeadsUp 展示了大规模数据、UV 参数化 Gaussian 表示与前馈架构结合在高质量 3D 头部重建中的有效性，并通过新身份生成和表情 blendshape 动画验证了潜空间的下游应用价值。

Abstract: We propose HeadsUp, a scalable feed-forward method for reconstructing high-quality 3D Gaussian heads from large-scale multi-camera setups. Our method employs an efficient encoder-decoder architecture that compresses input views into a compact latent representation. This latent representation is then decoded into a set of UV-parameterized 3D Gaussians anchored to a neutral head template. This UV representation decouples the number of 3D Gaussians from the number and resolution of input images, enabling training with many high-resolution input views. We train and evaluate our model on an internal dataset with more than 10,000 subjects, which is an order of magnitude larger than existing multi-view human head datasets. HeadsUp achieves state-of-the-art reconstruction quality and generalizes to novel identities without test-time optimization. We extensively analyze the scaling behavior of our model across identities, views, and model capacity, revealing practical insights for quality-compute trade-offs. Finally, we highlight the strength of our latent space by showcasing two downstream applications: generating novel 3D identities and animating the 3D heads with expression blendshapes.

### [62] [Large Language Models are Universal Reasoners for Visual Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04040)
*Sucheng Ren,Chen Chen,Zhenbang Wang,Liangchen Song,Xiangxin Zhu,Alan Yuille,Liang-Chieh Chen,Jiasen Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 UniReasoner，利用 LLM 的理解与自我评估能力为文本到图像扩散生成提供显式纠错指导，从而缓解复杂提示下的理解-生成差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管统一式文本到图像系统已能用单一 LLM 骨干同时处理视觉理解与生成，但其在复杂提示合成时仍常出现语义遗漏、关系错误或幻觉；与此同时，这些模型却能较准确地判断图像是否满足同一提示。论文将这种现象定义为“理解-生成差距”，目标是把 LLM 的验证/理解能力转化为生成过程中的有效约束。

Method: UniReasoner 包含三步：首先，LLM 根据输入提示生成由离散视觉 token 构成的粗略视觉草稿；其次，LLM 对该草稿进行自我批判，评估其与提示的一致性，并输出有依据的文本评价，指出需要修正的内容；最后，扩散模型同时以原始提示、视觉草稿和评价文本为条件进行图像生成。视觉草稿提供场景级锚点，评价文本提供可操作的纠错信号。

Result: 实验表明，在使用相同扩散骨干的情况下，UniReasoner 提升了组合式对齐能力和语义忠实度，同时保持了图像质量。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了通过让 LLM 先构建视觉草稿并进行自我评估，可以将其理解与验证能力转化为生成指导，从而有效缩小文本到图像任务中的理解-生成差距。

Abstract: Text-to-image generation has advanced rapidly with diffusion models, progressing from CLIP and T5 conditioning to unified systems where a single LLM backbone handles both visual understanding and generation. Despite the architectural unification, these systems frequently fail to faithfully align complex prompts during synthesis, even though they remain highly accurate at verifying whether an image satisfies those same prompts. We formalize this as the \emph{understanding-generation gap} and propose UniReasoner, a framework that leverages the LLM as a universal reasoner to convert its understanding strength into direct generation guidance. Given a prompt, the LLM first produces a coarse visual draft composed of discrete vision tokens. It then performs a self-critique by evaluating the draft for prompt consistency, producing a grounded textual evaluation that pinpoints what needs to be corrected. Finally, a diffusion model is conditioned jointly on the prompt, the visual draft, and the evaluation, ensuring that generation is guided by explicit corrective signals. Each signal addresses a limitation of the other: the draft provides a concrete, scene-level anchor that reduces under-specification in text-only conditioning, while the evaluation turns verification into grounded, actionable constraints that correct omissions, hallucinations, and relational errors. Experiments show that UniReasoner improves compositional alignment and semantic faithfulness under the same diffusion backbone while maintaining image quality, demonstrating a practical way to exploit LLM reasoning to close the understanding-generation gap.

</details>


### [63] [UniCorrn: Unified Correspondence Transformer Across 2D and 3D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04044)
*Prajnan Goswami,Tianye Ding,Feng Liu,Huaizu Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: UniCorrn 是一个共享权重的统一几何匹配模型，可同时处理 2D-2D、2D-3D 和 3D-3D 对应关系任务，并在 2D-3D 与 3D-3D 注册召回上显著优于既有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉/几何对应方法通常针对不同模态组合分别设计模型，导致模型割裂、参数不共享、跨任务泛化与统一建模能力不足。论文希望利用这些任务共同的对应关系结构，构建一个可跨图像与点云模态统一工作的匹配框架。

Method: 论文提出 UniCorrn，使用模态特定 backbone 提取初始特征，随后采用共享的 encoder 与 dual-stream decoder。双流解码器分别维护 appearance feature stream 与 positional feature stream，通过 Transformer attention 捕获跨模态特征相似性，并支持基于 query 的灵活对应估计。训练上联合使用由深度图生成的伪点云数据以及真实 3D 对应标注。

Result: UniCorrn 在 2D-2D 匹配上达到有竞争力的性能；在 7Scenes 的 2D-3D 任务中注册召回率相比先前最优方法提升 8%；在 3DLoMatch 的 3D-3D 任务中注册召回率提升 10%。

Conclusion: 该工作表明 Transformer attention 可作为统一跨模态几何对应建模的有效机制；通过共享权重与双流解码设计，单一模型能够覆盖多种几何匹配任务，并在部分 3D 视觉基准上取得领先表现。

Abstract: Visual correspondence across image-to-image (2D-2D), image-to-point cloud (2D-3D), and point cloud-to-point cloud (3D-3D) geometric matching forms the foundation for numerous 3D vision tasks. Despite sharing a similar problem structure, current methods use task-specific designs with separate models for each modality combination. We present UniCorrn, the first correspondence model with shared weights that unifies geometric matching across all three tasks. Our key insight is that Transformer attention naturally captures cross-modal feature similarity. We propose a dual-stream decoder that maintains separate appearance and positional feature streams. This design enables end-to-end learning through stack-able layers while supporting flexible query-based correspondence estimation across heterogeneous modalities. Our architecture employs modality-specific backbones followed by shared encoder and decoder components, trained jointly on diverse data combining pseudo point clouds from depth maps with real 3D correspondence annotations. UniCorrn achieves competitive performance on 2D-2D matching and surpasses prior state-of-the-art by 8% on 7Scenes (2D-3D) and 10% on 3DLoMatch (3D-3D) in registration recall. Project website: https://neu-vi.github.io/UniCorrn

</details>


### [64] [Audio-Visual Intelligence in Large Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04045)
*You Qin,Kai Liu,Shengqiong Wu,Kai Wang,Shijian Deng,Yapeng Tian,Junbin Xiao,Yazhou Xing,Yinghao Ma,Bobo Li,Roger Zimmermann,Lei Cui,Furu Wei,Jiebo Luo,Hao Fei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文是一篇面向大基础模型时代的音视频智能（AVI）综述，提出统一分类体系，系统梳理任务、方法、数据集、评测与开放挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文从大基础模型视角构建 AVI 统一综述框架：覆盖理解、生成、交互等任务族；总结模态标记化、跨模态融合、自回归与扩散式生成、大规模预训练、指令对齐和偏好优化等关键方法；并整理代表性数据集、基准和评价指标。

Result: 该综述形成了对 AVI 领域的结构化归纳，提供跨任务族的比较视角，并识别出同步性、空间推理、可控性与安全性等核心开放问题。

Abstract: Audio-Visual Intelligence (AVI) has emerged as a central frontier in artificial intelligence, bridging auditory and visual modalities to enable machines that can perceive, generate, and interact in the multimodal real world. In the era of large foundation models, joint modeling of audio and vision has become increasingly crucial, i.e., not only for understanding but also for controllable generation and reasoning across dynamic, temporally grounded signals. Recent advances, such as Meta MovieGen and Google Veo-3, highlight the growing industrial and academic focus on unified audio-vision architectures that learn from massive multimodal data. However, despite rapid progress, the literature remains fragmented, spanning diverse tasks, inconsistent taxonomies, and heterogeneous evaluation practices that impede systematic comparison and knowledge integration. This survey provides the first comprehensive review of AVI through the lens of large foundation models. We establish a unified taxonomy covering the broad landscape of AVI tasks, ranging from understanding (e.g., speech recognition, sound localization) to generation (e.g., audio-driven video synthesis, video-to-audio) and interaction (e.g., dialogue, embodied, or agentic interfaces). We synthesize methodological foundations, including modality tokenization, cross-modal fusion, autoregressive and diffusion-based generation, large-scale pretraining, instruction alignment, and preference optimization. Furthermore, we curate representative datasets, benchmarks, and evaluation metrics, offering a structured comparison across task families and identifying open challenges in synchronization, spatial reasoning, controllability, and safety. By consolidating this rapidly expanding field into a coherent framework, this survey aims to serve as a foundational reference for future research on large-scale AVI.

### [65] [When Should a Language Model Trust Itself? Same-Model Self-Verification as a Conditional Confidence Signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02915)
*Aditya Ajay Phalod*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文评估同模型自验证作为选择性预测置信信号的有效性，发现其并非通用不确定性估计器，而是依赖任务、模型、提示和基线的条件性信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同模型自验证让模型审计自身答案，直观上可作为置信度信号；但在与强似然基线（LL-AVG、LL-SUM）比较时，其实际价值仍不明确。

Method: 作者在 ARC-Challenge 与 TruthfulQA-MC 上，跨多个模型家族、模型规模和提示变体，将自验证与 LL-AVG、LL-SUM 进行比较；评估指标包括正确性排序、AURC 以及不同操作点下的拒答/选择性预测质量。

Result: 结果呈现明显的任务和模型依赖性：在 ARC-Challenge 上，自验证相较 LL-AVG 对 Phi-2 和 Qwen 系列有显著提升，Qwen-7B 提升最大；在 TruthfulQA-MC 上，自验证不稳定，小模型对提示敏感，DeepSeek-R1-Distill-8B 相比 LL-AVG 退化，LL-SUM 往往仍是更强的实用基线。

Conclusion: 自验证不应被视为通用置信度或不确定性估计方法，而应理解为一种条件性置信信号，其价值取决于任务类型、模型家族、提示设计以及需要超越的基线。

Abstract: Same-model self-verification, prompting a model to audit its own predicted answer, is a plausible confidence signal for selective prediction, but its practical value remains unclear once strong likelihood-based baselines are taken seriously. We evaluate self-verification against two such baselines, LL-AVG and LL-SUM, on ARC-Challenge and TruthfulQA-MC across multiple model families, scales, and prompt variants. We measure not only correctness ranking, but also abstention quality through AURC and operating-point analyses. The results are sharply task- and model-dependent. On ARC-Challenge, self-verification substantially improves over LL-AVG for Phi-2 and the Qwen models, with the largest gains appearing in Qwen-7B. On TruthfulQA-MC, however, the signal is less reliable: smaller models can become prompt-sensitive, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-8B degrades relative to LL-AVG, and LL-SUM often remains the stronger practical baseline. We therefore do not treat self-verification as a general-purpose uncertainty estimator. In this setting, it is better understood as a conditional confidence signal whose value depends on task type, model family, prompt formulation, and, crucially, the baseline it must beat.

</details>


### [66] [Evaluating Reasoning Models for Queries with Presuppositions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03050)
*Rose Sathyanathan,Kinshuk Vasisht,Danish Pruthi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文评估大型推理模型在面对带有错误预设的问题时，是否能识别并纠正其中的虚假前提；结果显示推理模型虽略优于非推理模型，但仍经常未能挑战错误预设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大量用户依赖 AI 模型获取信息，而用户问题中可能包含事实错误的隐含假设。既有研究发现 LLM 往往不会质疑这些错误前提，甚至可能强化误解。随着推理能力更强的模型出现，作者希望重新检验大型推理模型是否能更好地识别问题背后的预设并作出恰当回应。

Method: 作者构建了一组包含不同强度预设的问题，覆盖健康、科学与通用知识领域，并用这些查询评估多个广泛部署的模型；同时比较推理模型与非推理模型在识别、挑战错误预设方面的表现，并分析预设表达强度对模型响应的影响。

Result: 与非推理模型相比，推理模型准确率仅提高约 2%–11%。然而，它们仍未能挑战相当比例的错误预设，失败率约为 26%–42%。此外，推理模型仍会受到预设表达强度的影响：错误前提表达得越强，模型越可能被误导。

Conclusion: 大型推理模型在处理含错误预设的问题时有一定改进，但远未可靠。推理能力并不能完全解决模型默认接受用户问题前提的问题，未来仍需加强模型对隐含假设的识别、质疑与纠错能力。

Abstract: Millions of users turn to AI models for their information needs. It is conceivable that a large number of user queries contain assumptions that may be factually inaccurate. Prior work notes that large language models (LLMs) often fail to challenge such erroneous assumptions, and can reinforce users' misinformed opinions. However, given the recent advances, especially in model's reasoning capabilities, we revisit whether large reasoning models (LRMs) can reason about the underlying assumptions and respond to user queries appropriately. We construct queries with varying degrees of presuppositions spanning health, science, and general knowledge, and use it to evaluate several widely-deployed models When compared to non-reasoning models, we find that reasoning models achieve a slightly higher accuracy (2-11%), but they still fail to challenge a large fraction (26-42%) of false presuppositions. Further, reasoning models remain susceptible to how strongly the presupposition is expressed.

</details>


### [67] [How Language Models Process Negation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03052)
*Zhejian Zhou,Tianyi Zhou,Robin Jia,Jonathan May*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型如何在机制层面处理否定，发现模型内部具备正确处理否定的组件，但最终错误常由后层注意力的捷径行为导致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管开放权重大语言模型在涉及否定的问题上常回答错误，但尚不清楚这是因为模型缺乏否定理解能力，还是因为内部存在正确机制但被其他计算路径干扰。论文旨在解释LLM处理否定的内部机制。

Method: 作者在 Mistral-7B 和 Llama-3.1-8B 上使用观察性与因果性可解释性技术，分析否定相关任务中的内部表示与注意力头行为；同时比较两种机制假设：通过注意被否定短语并抑制相关概念，或直接构造整个否定短语的表示。

Result: 研究发现模型内部确实存在能正确处理否定的组件；错误主要源于后层注意力模块倾向于强化简单捷径。消融这些注意力模块能显著提升否定问题准确率。模型同时使用抑制机制和构造机制，其中构造负短语表示的机制更突出。

Conclusion: LLM对否定的处理并非单一失败，而是内部存在正确与错误计算路径的竞争。模型更倾向于通过构造完整否定短语表示来处理否定，这加深了对LLM内部机制、构造性计算以及多机制共存现象的理解。

Abstract: We study how Large Language Models (LLMs) process negation mechanistically. First, we establish that even though open-weight models often provide wrong answers to questions involving negation, they do possess internal components that process negation correctly. Their poor accuracy is due to late-layer attention behavior that promotes simple shortcuts; ablating those attention modules greatly improves accuracy on negation-related questions. Second, we uncover how models process negation. We consider two hypotheses: models could use attention heads that attend to the phrase being negated and suppress related concepts, or they could directly construct a representation of the entire negative phrase (e.g., representing "not gas" as a vector that promotes liquids and solids). We apply a range of observational and causal interpretability techniques on Mistral-7B and Llama-3.1-8B to show that models implement both mechanisms, with the "constructive" mechanism being more prominent. Combined, our work deepens the understanding of LLMs' internals, highlighting construction-dominant computations and the coexistence of competing mechanisms within LLMs.

</details>


### [68] [The TTS-STT Flywheel: Synthetic Entity-Dense Audio Closes the Indic ASR Gap Where Commercial and Open-Source Systems Fail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03073)
*Venkata Pushpak Teja Menta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种面向小众实体密集场景的 Indic ASR 自举流程，通过低成本合成实体密集语料并进行 LoRA 微调，显著提升 Telugu/Hindi/Tamil 的实体识别命中率，但仍未达到预注册目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源与商业 ASR 在 Indic 语言的特定实体场景中表现不足，例如数字串、金额、地址、品牌名以及英语/Indic 代码混合内容，尤其在 Telugu 等语言上实体识别能力很弱。

Method: 构建自包含 TTS↔STT flywheel：使用开源 Indic TTS 合成约 2.2 万条实体密集 Indic-English code-mix 语音，成本低于 50 美元；在 vasista22/whisper-telugu-large-v2 上进行 LoRA 微调，并在 Telugu、Hindi、Tamil beta 模型上评估。包含合成测试集、人类录音 sanity check、FLEURS 回归测试、EDSA 隔离消融及脚本保真率分析。

Conclusion: 该工作证明低成本合成实体密集语料结合 LoRA 微调可显著改善 Indic ASR 在小众实体场景中的表现，并通过开源发布增强可复现性；但模型仍低于预注册 EHR 目标，且方法对语言条件敏感，在 Hindi/Tamil 中并非总优于强商业系统或原始模型。

Abstract: Niche-domain Indic ASR -- digit strings, currency amounts, addresses, brand names, English/Indic codemix -- is under-served by both open-source SOTA and commercial systems. On a synthesised entity-dense Telugu test set (held-out by synthesis system), vasista22/whisper-telugu-large-v2 (open SOTA) achieves Entity-Hit-Rate (EHR) 0.027 and Deepgram Nova-3 (commercial) 0.16. We close this gap with a self-contained TTS<->STT flywheel: an open-source Indic TTS pipeline synthesises ~22,000 entity-dense Indic-English code-mix utterances at <$50 marginal cost, and a LoRA fine-tune on top of vasista22 achieves EHR 0.473 on the held-out test (17x over open SOTA, 3x over commercial), with read-prose regression bounded to +6.6 pp WER on FLEURS-Te. Cross-language: beta-Hi 0.337 (7x vs vasista22) and beta-Ta 0.543 (22x vs vasista22, 22x vs Deepgram); on Hindi where Deepgram has substantial entity coverage, the flywheel underperforms commercial. All three beta models fall below pre-registered EHR targets (0.75 for Te, 0.65 for Hi/Ta); we report honestly. A native-human-recorded sanity check (n=20 Telugu) confirms transfer to real speech (beta-Te EHR 0.516 on native vs 0.473 on synth). An EDSA-isolation ablation (LoRA on FLEURS-Te alone) yields EHR 0.020 on the same held-out, attributing ~100% of the gain to the EDSA corpus. We additionally report a language-conditional finding: vanilla Whisper-large-v3 has Telugu-specific Script Collapse (SFR 0.46-0.71) that a per-language LoRA corrects (SFR 0.81-0.97), but the recipe is contraindicated on Hindi and Tamil where vanilla SFR >= 0.98. Code, holdouts, predictions, EDSA corpus, and entity dictionaries are released open-source.

Result: 编码器-only模型在非空值键条件问答上表现最佳，且规模显著小于解码器-only模型；在相近参数量级比较时，编码器-only模型整体更优；若不控制模型规模，微调后的解码器-only模型取得最强总体结果。

Abstract: Semi-structured information extraction (IE) from OCR-derived clinical reports is crucial for efficiently reconstructing patients' longitudinal medical histories. However, existing evaluations often under-model two factors: heterogeneous and incompletely known key representations, and OCR-induced noise. This makes it difficult to assess model robustness in real-world settings.
  We present MedStruct-S, a benchmark specifically designed to evaluate these tasks under unknown keys and OCR noise. MedStruct-S contains 3,582 annotated real-world clinical report pages. Using MedStruct-S, we benchmark two representative paradigms: encoder-only sequence labeling with post-processing and decoder-only structured generation, covering four encoder-only and five decoder-only models spanning 0.11B to 103B parameters. Our results show that encoder-only models achieve the best performance for non-null-value key-conditioned QA despite being substantially smaller than decoder-only models. When comparing models of similar order of magnitude, encoder-only models still perform better overall. Without controlling for model scale, fine-tuned decoder-only models deliver the strongest overall results. These findings show that the benchmark provides a reliable and practical basis for selecting and comparing models across different semi-structured IE settings.

### [71] [Geometric Deviation as an Unsupervised Pre-Generation Reliability Signal: Probing LLM Representations for Answerability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03196)
*Yucheng Du*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究隐藏状态的表示几何是否能在生成前预测问题是否超出模型可回答范围；结果显示该信号在数学等结构化任务中有效，但在事实类提示中不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的语言模型应在生成前识别不可回答或超出知识范围的问题。现有方法往往依赖模型输出、拒答行为或标注失败数据，成本较高且可能滞后，因此作者希望寻找一种无需生成、无需失败标签的轻量级预生成检测信号。

Method: 作者构建可回答参考集，测量待测提示在模型隐藏状态空间中相对该参考集质心的几何偏离程度。实验覆盖三个指令微调模型（Llama 3.1-8B、Qwen 2.5-7B、Mistral-7B-Instruct）和三类提示形式（数学、事实、代码），并进行ROC-AUC评估、与拒答基线和自一致性比较，以及逐层分析。

Result: 表示几何主要编码任务形式。在数学提示中，不可回答输入稳定偏离可回答质心，区分效果较强（ROC-AUC 0.78–0.84），优于简单拒答基线，并接近或优于自一致性，同时能捕捉模型未显式拒答的失败案例。事实类提示未出现可靠几何信号；代码提示效果量较大但方差更高。逐层分析表明信号在早期层出现，并向输出层逐渐衰减。

Conclusion: 几何偏离可作为结构化领域中判断可回答性的轻量级预生成信号，尤其适用于具有形式化可回答约束的数学任务；但其泛化具有明确边界，在事实类任务中并不稳定，因此不能视为通用不可回答检测方法。

Abstract: A reliable language model should be able to signal, prior to generation, when a query falls outside its knowledge. We investigate whether representation geometry can provide such a pre-generation signal by measuring the deviation of hidden states from an answerable reference set, requiring no labeled failure data and no access to model outputs. Across three instruction-tuned models (Llama 3.1-8B, Qwen 2.5-7B, and Mistral-7B-Instruct) and three prompt forms (Math, Fact, Code), we find that geometry primarily encodes task form. Within mathematical prompts, unanswerable inputs consistently deviate from the answerable centroid, yielding strong separation (ROC-AUC 0.78-0.84). This single-pass pre-generation signal outperforms a simple refusal baseline and compares favorably to self-consistency. It also captures cases where models do not explicitly refuse. In contrast, no reliable geometric signal emerges for factual prompts, indicating that the effect is form-conditional rather than universal. Code prompts show large effect sizes with higher variance, suggesting partial generalization beyond mathematical form. A layer-wise analysis reveals that the signal arises in early layers and gradually attenuates toward the output. These results suggest that answerability-related geometry is established before the final stages of generation. Together, these findings indicate that geometric deviation can serve as a lightweight pre-generation signal that is reliable in structured domains with formal answerability constraints, with clear boundaries on where it generalizes.

### [72] [S^2tory: Story Spine Distillation for Movie Script Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03244)
*Mingzhe Lu,Yanbing Liu,Qihao Wang,Jiarui Zhang,Jiayue Wu,Yue Hu,Yunpeng Li,Yangyan Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 S^2tory（Story Spine Distillation），用叙事学中的角色发展轨迹来识别推动剧情的核心事件，并据此生成电影剧本摘要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电影剧本具有非线性、交叉剪辑式叙事结构，传统基于表层显著性的摘要方法难以保留核心故事推进逻辑，因此需要一种更贴合叙事机制的摘要框架。

Method: 框架先由 Narrative Expert Agent（NEAgent）进行受叙事理论约束的推理，识别角色发展轨迹中的 plot nuclei（推动叙事前进的关键事件），过滤 satellite events（氛围或情绪补充事件）；随后将该知识蒸馏到小模型中用于核心事件识别，再由另一个模型基于这些核心事件生成摘要。

Result: 在 MovieSum 数据集上，该方法在约 3.5 倍压缩率下取得语义保真度的当前最优表现；在 BookSum 上的零样本评估显示出较强的领域外泛化能力；人工评估也支持其叙事理论建模的有效性。

Conclusion: 叙事学理论，尤其是基于角色发展轨迹的故事主干建模，有助于处理复杂、非线性叙事文本的自动摘要，并能提升摘要的语义保真度与泛化能力。

Abstract: Movie scripts pose a fundamental challenge for automatic summarization due to their non-linear, cross-cut narrative structure, which makes surface-level saliency methods ineffective at preserving core story progression. To address this, we introduce S^2tory (Story Spine Distillation), a narratology-grounded framework that leverages character development trajectories to identify plot nuclei, the essential events that drive the narrative forward, while filtering out peripheral satellite events that merely enrich atmosphere or emotion. Our Narrative Expert Agent (NEAgent) performs theory-constrained reasoning, whose distilled knowledge conditions a small model to identify plot nuclei. Another model then uses these plot nuclei to generate the summary. Experiments on the MovieSum dataset demonstrate state-of-the-art semantic fidelity at approximately 3.5x compression, and zero-shot evaluation on BookSum confirms strong out-of-domain generalization. Human evaluation further validates that narratological theory provides an indispensable foundation for modeling complex, non-linear narratives.

### [73] [LLM-XTM: Enhancing Cross-Lingual Topic Models with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03299)
*Minh Chu Xuan,Tien-Phat Nguyen,Linh Ngo Van,Dinh Viet Sang,Nguyen Thi Ngoc Diep,Trung Le*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文提出 LLM-XTM 框架：在传统跨语言主题模型基础上，引入 LLM 指导的主题精炼，并利用自一致性进行不确定性量化，从而在黑盒 LLM 场景下筛选或稳定主题增强结果，减少对内部概率信息和大量双语词典的依赖。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，通过黑盒 LLM 精炼与自一致性不确定性估计结合，可以更稳定、经济且可扩展地增强跨语言主题模型，缓解传统资源稀缺和 LLM 幻觉/成本问题。

Abstract: Cross-lingual topic modeling aims to discover shared semantic structures across languages, yet existing models depend on sparse bilingual resources and often yield incoherent or weakly aligned topics. Recent LLM-based refinements improve interpretability but are costly, document-level, and prone to hallucination, with prior white-box approaches requiring inaccessible token probabilities. We propose LLM-XTM, a framework that integrates LLM-guided topic refinement with self-consistency uncertainty quantification, enabling black-box, stable, and scalable enhancement of cross-lingual topic models. Experiments on multilingual corpora show that LLM-XTM achieves superior topic coherence and alignment while reducing reliance on bilingual dictionaries and expensive LLM calls.

### [74] [SHIELD: A Diverse Clinical Note Dataset and Distilled Small Language Models for Enterprise-Scale De-identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03301)
*Jose D. Posada,David Love,Somalee Datta,Priya Desai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出并发布SHIELD临床文本去标识化数据集，并通过LLM到SLM的蒸馏实现可本地部署的高性能PHI识别模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有公开临床去标识化基准年代久远，难以覆盖现代EHR叙事的语义与人群多样性；同时LLM虽具备强零样本能力，但云端API成本与PHI治理限制阻碍其企业部署。

Method: 构建包含1,394条临床笔记、10,505个人工金标准PHI跨度、9类PHI的SHIELD数据集；采用集合覆盖多样性采样与人机协同裁决；评估4个LLM作为性能上限，并将其能力蒸馏到本地可部署的小语言模型；用Frechet Text Distance与Jensen-Shannon Divergence分析与旧基准的数据分布差异。

Result: SHIELD在生物医学嵌入和词汇空间中与旧基准分布明显不同；最佳蒸馏模型在DATE、DOCTOR、ID、PATIENT、PHONE等结构化PHI类别上匹配教师模型，并在标准工作站硬件上达到微平均跨度级precision 0.88、recall 0.86；跨数据集评估显示多样性训练提升通用结构化PHI泛化，但机构特异实体迁移仍困难。

Conclusion: SHIELD补足了现代临床去标识化公开基准的不足，LLM蒸馏到SLM可在隐私与成本受限场景中实现实用部署；最佳策略可能是广覆盖基础模型结合面向高频笔记或机构特异实体的专门模型。

Abstract: De-identification of clinical text remains essential for secondary use of electronic health records (EHRs), yet public benchmarks such as i2b2 2006/2014 are over a decade old and lack the semantic and demographic diversity of modern narratives. While Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve state-of-the-art zero-shot extraction, enterprise deployment is hindered by compute costs and governance restricting Protected Health Information (PHI) from cloud APIs. We introduce SHIELD (Synthetic Human-annotated Identifier-replaced Entries for Learning and De-identification), a diverse dataset of 1,394 notes with 10,505 gold-standard PHI spans across 9 categories, built via set-cover diversity sampling with human-in-the-loop adjudication. We evaluate four LLMs (two proprietary, two open-weight) to establish a performance ceiling, then distill these capabilities into locally deployable Small Language Models (SLMs). Distributional analysis using Frechet Text Distance and Jensen-Shannon Divergence confirms SHIELD occupies a distinct region of biomedical embedding and vocabulary space versus legacy benchmarks. Our best distilled model matches its teacher on structured PHI categories (DATE, DOCTOR, ID, PATIENT, PHONE) and achieves micro-averaged span-level precision of 0.88 and recall of 0.86 on standard workstation hardware. Cross-dataset evaluation shows diversity-trained models generalize well on universal structured PHI, while institution-specific entities remain hard to transfer, suggesting optimal deployment combines broad-coverage models with specialized models for high-volume notes. We publicly release the SHIELD dataset and the distilled DeBERTa v3 model.

</details>


### [75] [From prompting to evidence-based translation: A RAG+prompt system for Japanese-Chinese translation and its pedagogical potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03387)

Mean BLEU increases from 24.28 at 0 (RAG disabled) to 29.96 at 2,000 (+5.68; +23.4%). The upward trend holds across sizes, with larger knowledge bases yielding higher scores.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: ASD儿童P200波幅显著降低且缺乏典型的后部语法性效应；两组均未出现稳健N400违反效应，但ASD儿童表现出反向前部效应和减弱的后部效应；P600阶段ASD儿童波幅降低、缺乏后部语法性效应，并呈现潜伏期延迟趋势。

Abstract: Recursive structures are a core property of human language, yet little is known about how children with autism spectrum disorder (ASD) process complex recursion. This ERP study investigated the online processing of two-level recursive possessive structures in Mandarin-speaking children with ASD (n = 12) compared to typically developing (TD) peers (n = 12) using a sentence-picture matching paradigm. ERPs were analyzed for P200 (150-250 ms), N400 (300-500 ms), and P600 (500-1000 ms). Results showed that ASD children exhibited significantly reduced P200 amplitudes and failed to show the typical posterior grammaticality effect, indicating atypical early perceptual processing. No robust N400 violation effect was observed in either group, confirming the mismatch was not a semantic anomaly; however, ASD children showed a reversed anterior effect and an attenuated posterior effect. For the P600, ASD children had significantly reduced amplitudes, no posterior grammaticality effect, and a trend toward delayed latency, reflecting a core deficit in syntactic reanalysis. These findings demonstrate that while lexical-semantic processing is relatively preserved in ASD, the online syntactic computation required for recursion is severely impaired, supporting modular dissociation accounts of language in autism.

In this study, we investigate how to employ Topic Models as binary classifiers for refining the retrieval of relevant news about seven types of extreme climate events in the German media. ### [81] [Detecting Stealth Sycophancy in Mental-Health Dialogue with Dynamic Emotional Signature Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03472)

We use a direct LLM judge as a baseline that reads raw dialogue text and predicts whether the target response is harmful, productive, or neutral. We find that direct LLM judges and symmetric text-similarity metrics are poorly aligned with therapeutic quality because the target label depends on clinical direction: whether the response moves the user state toward regulation or reframing, leaves it broadly unchanged, or reinforces deterioration through higher risk affect or cognitive-distortion mass. To address this issue, we propose Dynamic Emotional Signature Graphs (DESG), a model-agnostic evaluator that represents dialogue windows with decoupled clinical states and scores them using asymmetric clinical geometry. On the 600-window held-out test aggregate, DESG-Ensemble achieves 0.9353 macro-F1, exceeding ConcatANN by 1.51 percentage points, BERTScore by 19.63 points, and TRACT by 33.81 points. ### [82] [CuraView: A Multi-Agent Framework for Medical Hallucination Detection with GraphRAG-Enhanced Knowledge Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03476)
*Severin Ye,Xiao Kong,Xiaopeng He,Guangsu Yan,Dongsuk Oh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 CuraView，一个面向出院小结的多智能体事实一致性幻觉检测框架，利用 GraphRAG 构建患者级 EHR 知识图谱，并在句子级给出证据检索、证据等级分类与可解释证据链；在 Discharge-Me 子集上显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工撰写出院小结需要从冗长电子健康记录中提取关键信息，成本高且耗时。LLM 虽能提高生成效率，但容易产生与源记录矛盾的事实一致性幻觉，在临床文档场景中会带来严重安全风险，因此需要可解释、证据支撑的自动检测机制。

Method: CuraView 从患者级 EHR 构建 GraphRAG 知识图谱，设计闭环的生成—检测流程。系统对出院小结进行句子级证据检索，并将每个陈述按四级证据强度分类：从强支持到直接矛盾（E1–E4）。框架输出结构化、可解释的证据链，并微调 Qwen3-14B 作为检测模型。

Result: 在 Discharge-Me benchmark 的 250 名患者子集上评估，其中 50 名作为测试集。微调后的 Qwen3-14B 在安全关键的 E4 指标上达到 F1=0.831，召回率 90.9%，精确率 76.5%；在 E3+E4 上达到 F1=0.823，相比基础模型有 50.0% 的相对提升，并优于 RAGTruth-style 与 QAGS-style 基线。

Conclusion: 基于证据链的图检索验证能显著提升临床文档事实可靠性，同时生成可复用的标注数据，可用于后续模型训练与蒸馏。

Abstract: Discharge summaries require extracting critical information from lengthy electronic health records (EHRs), a process that is labor-intensive when performed manually. Large language models (LLMs) can improve generation efficiency; however, they are prone to producing faithfulness hallucinations, statements that contradict source records, posing direct risks to patient safety. To address this, we present CuraView, a multi-agent framework for sentence-level detection and evidence-grounded explanation of faithfulness hallucinations in discharge summaries. CuraView constructs a GraphRAG-based knowledge graph from patient-level EHRs and implements a closed-loop generation-detection pipeline with sentence-level evidence retrieval and classification spanning four evidence grades from strong support to direct contradiction (E1-E4), yielding structured and interpretable evidence chains.
  We evaluate CuraView on a subset of 250 patients from the Discharge-Me benchmark, with 50 patients held out for testing. Our fine-tuned Qwen3-14B detection model achieves an F1 of 0.831 on the safety-critical E4 metric (90.9% recall, 76.5% precision) and an F1 of 0.823 on E3+E4, representing a 50.0% relative improvement over the base model and outperforming RAGTruth-style and QAGS-style baselines. These results demonstrate that evidence-chain-based graph retrieval verification substantially improves the factual reliability of clinical documentation, while simultaneously producing reusable annotated datasets for downstream model training and distillation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型被广泛用于图任务，GTokenLLMs通过将图压缩为图令牌并作为前缀输入LLM，被认为能更高效理解图结构。但作者怀疑这些模型是否真的在自然语言嵌入空间中理解图令牌。

Method: 作者形式化了GTokenLLMs的统一框架，并提出GTEval评估流水线，从格式层面和内容层面对指令进行变换，以测试模型对图令牌的理解能力；同时在6种代表性GTokenLLMs上开展实验分析。

Result: 实验发现：现有GTokenLLMs并未充分理解图令牌；它们对指令变化表现出过度敏感或过度不敏感，并严重依赖文本信息进行推理；图令牌虽然保留任务相关图信息并在LLM层中获得注意力，但不同模型和指令变体中的利用程度差异明显；额外指令微调可提升原始和已见指令上的性能，但不能根本解决图令牌理解问题。

Conclusion: 现有Graph-Tokenizing LLMs距离真正理解和稳健利用图令牌仍有差距，需要新的建模、对齐或训练方法来提升其图结构理解能力和跨指令泛化能力。

Abstract: The remarkable success of large language models (LLMs) has motivated researchers to adapt them as universal predictors for various graph tasks. As a widely recognized paradigm, Graph-Tokenizing LLMs (GTokenLLMs) compress complex graph data into graph tokens and treat them as prefix tokens for querying LLMs, leading many to believe that LLMs can understand graphs more effectively and efficiently. In this paper, we challenge this belief: \textit{Do GTokenLLMs fully understand graph tokens in the natural-language embedding space?} Motivated by this question, we formalize a unified framework for GTokenLLMs and propose an evaluation pipeline, \textbf{GTEval}, to assess graph-token understanding via instruction transformations at the format and content levels. We conduct extensive experiments on 6 representative GTokenLLMs with GTEval. The primary findings are as follows: (1) Existing GTokenLLMs do not fully understand graph tokens. They exhibit over-sensitivity or over-insensitivity to instruction changes, and rely heavily on text for reasoning; (2) Although graph tokens preserve task-relevant graph information and receive attention across LLM layers, their utilization varies across models and instruction variants; (3) Additional instruction tuning can improve performance on the original and seen instructions, but it does not fully address the challenge of graph-token understanding, calling for further improvement.

</details>


### [84] [SURE-RAG: Sufficiency and Uncertainty-Aware Evidence Verification for Selective Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03534)
*Jingxi Qiu,Zeyu Han,Cheng Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 SURE-RAG，用于判断检索证据是否足以支持候选答案，并在证据不足时选择拒答；在受控多跳 RAG 基准上取得高 Macro-F1 和更低风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG 中检索到相关段落并不等于答案被证据验证；单篇段落评分难以发现缺失推理跳、证据冲突或不确定检索，因此需要面向答案级别的证据充分性验证机制。

Method: 将任务定义为给定问题、候选答案和检索证据，预测支持、反驳或证据不足。SURE-RAG 使用共享的成对 claim-evidence 验证器生成局部关系分布，再聚合为覆盖度、关系强度、分歧、冲突和检索不确定性等可解释信号，形成三分类决策和可审计选择性评分。

Result: 在 HotpotQA-RAG v3 上，校准后的 SURE-RAG 达到 0.9075 Macro-F1（0.8951±0.0069），优于 DeBERTa mean-pooling 的 0.6516 和 GPT-4o judge 的 0.7284，并接近强但不透明的 concat cross-encoder（0.8888±0.0109）。30% 覆盖率下风险从 0.2588 降至 0.1642， unsafe answers 减少 37%。在 HaluBench unsafe detection 上与 GPT-4o 排名反转，说明两类任务不同。

Conclusion: SURE-RAG 表明证据充分性验证应作为集合级问题处理；其优势在于透明、可审计、选择性拒答能力强，适合受控 RAG 证据验证场景，但不能简单等同于开放式自然幻觉检测。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) grounds answers in retrieved passages, but retrieval is not verification: a passage can be topical and still fail to justify the answer. We frame this gap as evidence sufficiency verification for selective RAG answering: given a question, a candidate answer, and retrieved evidence, predict whether the evidence supports, refutes, or is insufficient, and abstain unless support is established. We present SURE-RAG, a transparent aggregation protocol built on the observation that evidence sufficiency is a set-level property: missing hops and unresolved conflicts cannot be detected by independent passage scoring. A shared pair-level claim-evidence verifier produces local relation distributions, which SURE-RAG aggregates into interpretable answer-level signals -- coverage, relation strength, disagreement, conflict, and retrieval uncertainty -- yielding a three-way decision and an auditable selective score. We evaluate on HotpotQA-RAG v3, a controlled multi-hop benchmark, under an artifact-aware protocol (shortcut baselines, counterfactual swaps, no-oracle checks, GPT-4o audits). Calibrated SURE-RAG reaches 0.9075 Macro-F1 (0.8951 +/- 0.0069), substantially above DeBERTa mean-pooling (0.6516) and a GPT-4o judge (0.7284), while matching a strong but opaque concat cross-encoder (0.8888 +/- 0.0109) with full auditability. Risk at 30% coverage drops from 0.2588 to 0.1642, a 37% reduction in unsafe answers. To deliberately probe the task boundary, we further contrast SURE-RAG with GPT-4o on HaluBench unsafe detection: the ranking reverses (0.3343 vs 0.7389 unsafe-F1), establishing that controlled sufficiency verification and natural hallucination detection are distinct problems.

</details>

### [90] [SERE: Structural Example Retrieval for Enhancing LLMs in Event Causality Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03701)
*Zhifeng Hao,Zhongjie Chen,Junhao Lu,Shengyin Yu,Guimin Hu,Keli Zhang,Ruichu Cai,Boyan Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 SERE，一种面向事件因果识别的结构化示例检索框架，通过检索更合适的 few-shot 示例来缓解大语言模型的因果幻觉并提升识别准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 事件因果识别要求判断上下文中两个事件是否存在因果关系。尽管大语言模型在多种 NLP 任务中表现良好，但在该任务中容易受到因果推理偏差影响，倾向于过度预测因果关系，产生因果幻觉。因此需要一种方法引导模型进行更可靠的因果判断。

Method: SERE 利用大语言模型的 few-shot learning 能力，设计结构化示例检索机制。该机制包含三类结构信息：基于 ConceptNet 中编辑距离的概念路径度量，用于衡量事件间概念关系；基于句法树编辑距离的句法度量，用于衡量上下文结构相似性；以及利用大语言模型按预定义因果结构筛选示例的因果模式过滤。最终选择与测试样本更相关的示例作为提示。

Result: 在多个事件因果识别数据集上的实验表明，SERE 能够有效提升大语言模型在 ECI 任务中的表现，并减轻因果关系过度预测问题。

Conclusion: 结构化示例检索能够为大语言模型提供更贴合任务需求的 few-shot 示例，从而改善事件因果推理的可靠性和准确性。SERE 证明了结合概念、句法与因果模式结构信息对 ECI 任务具有实际价值。

Abstract: Event Causality Identification (ECI) requires models to determine whether a given pair of events in a context exhibits a causal relationship. While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance across various NLP tasks, their effectiveness in ECI remains limited due to biases in causal reasoning, often leading to overprediction of causal relationships (causal hallucination). To mitigate these issues and enhance LLM performance in ECI, we propose SERE, a structural example retrieval framework that leverages LLMs' few-shot learning capabilities. SERE introduces an innovative retrieval mechanism based on three structural concepts: (i) Conceptual Path Metric, which measures the conceptual relationship between events using edit distance in ConceptNet; (ii) Syntactic Metric, which quantifies structural similarity through tree edit distance on syntactic trees; and (iii) Causal Pattern Filtering, which filters examples based on predefined causal structures using LLMs. By integrating these structural retrieval strategies, SERE selects more relevant examples to guide LLMs in causal reasoning, mitigating bias and improving accuracy in ECI tasks. Extensive experiments on multiple ECI datasets validate the effectiveness of SERE. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/DMIRLAB-Group/SERE.

### [91] [SAM-NER: Semantic Archetype Mediation for Zero-Shot Named Entity Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03706)
*Ruichu Cai,Juntao Gan,Miao Mai,Zhifeng Hao,Boyan Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SAM-NER 提出通过“语义原型中介”提升零样本命名实体识别在跨领域、跨标签体系场景下的稳健性，并在 CrossNER 上优于既有强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零样本 NER 在目标领域或标签体系变化时表现脆弱，原因是未见过的细粒度标签定义可能与 LLM 内部语义组织不一致，导致实体到目标标签的直接映射出现系统性语义漂移，尤其在新颖或语义重叠的标签体系中更明显。

Method: 论文提出三阶段框架 SAM-NER：首先进行实体发现，通过协作式抽取与基于共识的去噪获得高覆盖、高可信实体跨度；其次进行抽象中介，将实体投射到由高层本体抽象蒸馏得到的紧凑、领域不变的通用语义原型空间；最后进行语义校准，利用冻结 LLM 在约束条件与标签定义对齐的推理下，将原型级预测解析为目标领域类型。

Result: 在 CrossNER 基准上的实验表明，SAM-NER 在跨领域零样本设置中持续优于强先前 ZS-NER 基线。

Conclusion: 通过引入领域不变的中间语义原型空间，SAM-NER 缓解了直接细粒度标签映射中的语义漂移问题，为零样本 NER 的跨领域迁移提供了更稳定的解决方案。

Abstract: Zero-shot Named Entity Recognition (ZS-NER) remains brittle under domain and schema shifts, where unseen label definitions often misalign with a large language model's (LLM's) intrinsic semantic organization. As a result, directly mapping entity mentions to fine-grained target labels can induce systematic semantic drift, especially when target schemas are novel or semantically overlapping. We propose \textbf{SAM-NER}, a three-stage framework based on \emph{Semantic Archetype Mediation} that stabilizes cross-domain transfer through an intermediate, domain-invariant archetype space. SAM-NER: (i) performs \emph{Entity Discovery} via cooperative extraction and consensus-based denoising to obtain high-coverage, high-fidelity entity spans; (ii) conducts \emph{Abstract Mediation} by projecting entities into a compact set of universal semantic archetypes distilled from high-level ontological abstractions; and (iii) applies \emph{Semantic Calibration} to resolve archetype-level predictions into target-domain types through constrained, definition-aligned inference with a frozen LLM. Experiments on the CrossNER benchmark show that SAM-NER consistently outperforms strong prior ZS-NER baselines in cross-domain settings. Our implementation will be open-sourced at https://github.com/DMIRLAB-Group/SAM-NER.

### [92] [Rose-SQL: Role-State Evolution Guided Structured Reasoning for Multi-Turn Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03720)

### [95] [Reproducing Complex Set-Compositional Information Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03824)
*Vincent Degenhart,Dewi Timman,Arjen P. de Vries,Faegheh Hasibi,Mohanna Hoveyda*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂信息需求常包含集合组合约束，但现有检索模型可能依赖语义捷径而非真正执行约束推理。作者希望通过可复现评测和受控数据集，区分模型的语义匹配能力与组合约束满足能力。

Method: 作者复现实验并比较主要检索方法族及面向推理的检索方法，在QUEST与QUEST+Variants上评测；同时提出LIMIT+，通过任意属性谓词和约束满足构造相关性，降低预训练知识的影响，并按组合深度进行分层分析。

Result: 在QUEST上，最佳神经检索器Recall@100超过0.41，是BM25约0.20的两倍以上；但ReasonIR、Search-R1等推理方法并不稳定优于通用检索器。在LIMIT+上，QUEST中最强方法Recall@100从约0.42跌至低于0.02，而经典词法检索达到约0.96。组合深度增加时所有方法性能下降，稀疏代数和词法方法更稳定，稠密方法明显崩溃。

Conclusion: 现有神经检索方法在表面语义基准上表现强，但未必真正掌握集合组合约束；受控评测显示词法/稀疏方法在约束满足任务中更可靠。LIMIT+及代码释放有助于未来开展可复现、可控的组合检索评估。

Abstract: Complex information needs may involve set-compositional queries using conjunction, disjunction, and exclusion, yet it remains unclear whether current retrieval paradigms genuinely satisfy such constraints or exploit `semantic shortcuts'. We conduct a reproducibility study to benchmark major retrieval families and reasoning-targeted methods on QUEST and QUEST+Variants, and introduce LIMIT+, a controlled benchmark where relevance depends on arbitrary attribute predicates and constraint satisfaction, and less on pretrained knowledge. Our findings show that (i) on QUEST, the best neural retrievers achieve an effectiveness that is more than double what can be achieved with BM25 (Recall@100 ${>}$0.41 vs.\ 0.20), but reasoning-targeted methods like ReasonIR and Search-R1 do not outperform general-purpose retrievers uniformly; (ii) on LIMIT+, gains fail to transfer, where the strongest QUEST method collapses from Recall@100${\approx}$0.42 to below 0.02, while classic lexical retrieval gains to ${\sim}$0.96. Lastly, (iii) stratifying by compositional depth reveals a consistent degradation across all methods, where algebraic sparse and lexical methods show more stable performance while dense approaches collapse. Abstract: We introduce TRACE, a cross-domain engineering framework for trustworthy agentic AI in operationally critical domains. TRACE combines a four-layer reference architecture with an explicit classical-ML vs. LLM-validator split (L2a/L2b), a stateful orchestration-and-escalation policy (L3), and bounded human supervision (L4); a metrologically grounded trust-metric suite mapped to GUM/VIM/ISO 17025; and a Model-Parsimony principle quantified by the Computational Parsimony Ratio (CPR). Three instantiations--clinical decision support, industrial multi-domain operations, and a judicial AI assistant--transfer the samearchitecture and metrics across principally different governance contexts. The L2a/L2b separation makes the use of large language models a deliberate design decision rather than an architectural default, with parsimony quantified through CPR. TRACE introduces CPR as a first-class design principle in trustworthy-AI engineering.

### [97] [MCJudgeBench: A Benchmark for Constraint-Level Judge Evaluation in Multi-Constraint Instruction Following](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03858)
*Jaeyun Lee,Junyoung Koh,Zeynel Tok,Hunar Batra,Ronald Clark*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对 LLM judge 的评估多聚焦整体回答是否满足指令，难以揭示模型在多个独立约束上的细粒度判断能力与稳定性，尤其无法定位 partial/no 等少见标签上的失效模式。

Method: 构建包含指令、候选回答、显式约束列表、每个约束的 gold 标签（yes/partial/no）以及受控响应扰动的数据集；同时设计不同评估提示模板以测试 judge 稳定性。使用正确性指标和不一致性指标评估闭源与开源 LLM judges，并区分随机解码导致的内在不一致与提示/响应扰动导致的流程性不一致。

Result: 实验显示，LLM judge 的可靠性具有多维特征：整体表现强不代表在各类约束标签上都可靠，尤其对较少见的 partial 和 no 判断更薄弱；正确性更高的 judge 不一定不一致性更低；加入推理过程可提升正确性，但不一定稳定提升一致性。

Conclusion: LLM judge 的评估应从整体响应级扩展到约束级，以系统分析多约束指令遵循中的类别敏感性、扰动鲁棒性和稳定性失效模式。

Abstract: Multi-constraint instruction following requires verifying whether a response satisfies multiple individual requirements, yet LLM judges are often assessed only through overall-response judgments. We introduce MCJudgeBench, a benchmark for constraint-level judge evaluation in multi-constraint instruction following. Each instance includes an instruction, a candidate response, an explicit constraint list, per-constraint gold labels in {yes, partial, no}, and controlled response-side perturbations. The evaluation protocol further includes evaluation prompt variants to test judge stability. We evaluate proprietary and open-source LLM judges using both correctness and inconsistency metrics, distinguishing intrinsic inconsistency under stochastic decoding from procedural inconsistency under prompt and response perturbations. Our results show that judge reliability has multiple dimensions: strong overall performance does not guarantee equally reliable detection across label categories, especially for rarer partial and no cases. Judges with higher correctness do not always have lower inconsistency. Evaluation with reasoning improves correctness but does not uniformly improve stability. These findings motivate evaluating LLM judges at the constraint level to study these failure modes.

### [99] [Steer Like the LLM: Activation Steering that Mimics Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03907)
*Geert Heyman,Frederik Vandeputte*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出将提示词引导视为激活引导的一种形式，并通过训练可解释的 Prompt Steering Replacement（PSR）模型模仿提示词干预，从而缩小激活引导与提示词引导之间的性能差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型推理时可通过提示词或激活干预进行引导，但常见激活引导方法通常不如提示词方法有效。作者希望理解提示词引导的机制，并将其成功行为蒸馏为更简单、可解释的激活层模型。

Method: 作者首先分析提示词引导与现有激活引导方法的机制差异，发现提示词引导对不同 token 的干预强度具有显著差异。基于此，提出 PSR 模型：从模型激活中估计 token-specific steering coefficients，并训练其模仿提示词引导产生的干预效果。

Result: 在多个语言模型和三个引导基准上，PSR 模型优于已有激活引导方法；在控制高连贯性生成结果时优势尤其明显，并且在 AxBench 和 persona steering 任务上相较提示词方法也具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 提示词引导可以被更忠实地建模为一种 token 依赖的激活干预过程。通过学习提示词干预的 token 特异性模式，PSR 能提升激活引导效果，并增强方法的可解释性与实用性。

Abstract: Large language models can be steered at inference time through prompting or activation interventions, but activation steering methods often underperform compared to prompt-based approaches. We propose a framework that formulates prompt steering as a form of activation steering and investigates whether distilling successful prompt steering behavior into simpler, interpretable models can close this gap. Our analysis reveals that popular activation steering methods are not faithful to the mechanics of prompt steering, which applies strong interventions on some tokens while barely affecting others. Based on these insights, we introduce Prompt Steering Replacement (PSR) models that estimate token-specific steering coefficients from the activations themselves and are trained to imitate prompt-based interventions. Experiments on three steering benchmarks across multiple language models show that PSR models outperform existing activation steering methods, especially when controlling for high-coherence completions, and also compare favorably to prompting on AxBench and persona steering.

*Daniel Drucker,Kyle Mahowald*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究语言模型能否通过“反例生成—定义修复”的迭代链执行哲学概念分析；结果显示该循环很快出现收益递减，定义更冗长但准确性未提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 概念分析是哲学方法论的核心，通常通过提出定义并用反例修正定义来推进。作者希望检验语言模型是否能在迭代过程中持续进行高层次哲学推理，并评估其反例判断与人类专家判断的一致性。

Method: 研究覆盖20个概念，运行数千轮反例—修复循环：一个语言模型实例生成针对既有定义的反例，另一个实例据此修复定义，循环重复；同时由人类专家和语言模型评审对反例有效性进行判断，并比较二者一致性。

Result: 许多模型生成的反例被人类专家和模型评审判为无效；模型评审接受的反例数量约为人类的两倍。尽管如此，单项有效性判断在人类之间以及人类与模型之间呈中等一致性。延长迭代会使定义越来越冗长，但并不提升准确性；部分概念本身难以获得稳定定义。

Conclusion: 语言模型具备一定哲学推理能力，但反例—修复迭代链很快达到边际收益递减，难以通过更多轮次获得更准确的概念定义。该任务可作为评估语言模型能否维持高层次迭代哲学推理的有价值测试场景。

Abstract: Conceptual analysis -- proposing definitions and refining them through counterexamples -- is central to philosophical methodology. We study whether language models can perform this task through iterated analysis and repair chains: one model instance generates counterexamples to a proposed definition, another repairs the definition, and the process repeats. Across 20 concepts and thousands of counterexample-repair cycles, we find that, although many LM-generated counterexamples are judged invalid by both expert humans and an LM judge, the LM judge accepts roughly twice as many as humans do. Nonetheless, per-item validity judgments are moderately consistent across humans and between humans and the LM. We further find that extended iteration produces increasingly verbose definitions without improving accuracy. We also see that some concepts resist stable definitions in general. These findings suggest that while LMs can engage in philosophical reasoning, the counterexample-repair loop hits diminishing returns quickly and could be a fruitful test case for evaluating whether LMs can sustain high-level iterated philosophical reasoning.

</details>


### [102] [Logical Consistency as a Bridge: Improving LLM Hallucination Detection via Label Constraint Modeling between Responses and Self-Judgments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03971)
*Hao Mi,Qiang Sheng,Shaofei Wang,Beizhe Hu,Yifan Sun,Zhengjia Wang,Hengqi Zeng,Yang Li,Danding Wang,Juan Cao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 LaaB（Logical Consistency-as-a-Bridge），通过逻辑一致性将 LLM 幻觉检测中的神经特征与符号自判断结合起来，以提升事实性幻觉检测效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测方法通常只关注单一视角：要么利用模型内部/输出中的微观不确定性特征，要么通过提示诱导模型给出宏观自我判断。这两类方法割裂了隐式神经不确定性与显式符号推理之间的联系，未能利用二者的相互依赖关系。

Method: LaaB 引入“元判断”过程，将符号标签映射回特征空间；利用回答标签与元判断标签在语义上相同或相反的逻辑关系，构建神经特征与符号判断之间的桥梁。框架通过互学习对齐并融合双视角信号，从而进行更全面的幻觉检测。

Result: 作者在 4 个公开数据集、4 个大语言模型和 8 个基线方法上进行了实验，结果显示 LaaB 相比现有方法具有更优的幻觉检测性能。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，将隐式神经特征与显式符号自判断通过逻辑一致性机制进行联合建模，可以更有效地识别 LLM 的事实性幻觉，为更可靠的幻觉检测提供了新的框架思路。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are prone to factual hallucinations, risking their reliability in real-world applications. Existing hallucination detectors mainly extract micro-level intrinsic patterns for uncertainty quantification or elicit macro-level self-judgments through verbalized prompts. However, these methods address only a single facet of the hallucination, focusing either on implicit neural uncertainty or explicit symbolic reasoning, thereby treating these inherently coupled behaviors in isolation and failing to exploit their interdependence for a holistic view. In this paper, we propose LaaB (Logical Consistency-as-a-Bridge), a framework that bridges neural features and symbolic judgments for hallucination detection. LaaB introduces a "meta-judgment" process to map symbolic labels back into the feature space. By leveraging the inherent logical bridge where response and meta-judgment labels are either the same or opposite based on the self-judgment's semantics, LaaB aligns and integrates dual-view signals via mutual learning and enhances the hallucination detection. Extensive experiments on 4 public datasets, across 4 LLMs, against 8 baselines demonstrate the superiority of LaaB.

</details>


### [103] [EQUITRIAGE: A Fairness Audit of Gender Bias in LLM-Based Emergency Department Triage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03998)
*Richard J. Young,Alice M. Matthews*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 EQUITRIAGE，对五个大语言模型在急诊 ESI 分诊任务中的性别公平性进行反事实审计，发现所有模型均存在超过预设阈值的性别翻转率，且不同模型的偏差机制与干预效果显著不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 急诊分诊中的病情严重度评分直接影响治疗优先级，而既有临床证据显示人工评估存在持续的性别差异。随着医院尝试使用大语言模型辅助分诊，亟需评估这些模型是否会复制、放大或缓解既有偏差。

Method: 研究在 18,714 个 MIMIC-IV-ED 病例文本上进行 374,275 次评估，覆盖五个 LLM 和四种提示策略；其中 9,346 个原始病例构造成性别互换的反事实配对。作者衡量 ESI 评分翻转率、方向性低分诊比例、组内校准、反事实不变性，并测试人口学信息遮蔽、保留年龄的遮蔽、链式思维提示以及 name+gender 与 gender token 的消融。

Result: 五个模型的反事实翻转率均超过预注册 5% 阈值，范围为 9.9%–43.8%。DeepSeek 与 Gemini 显示女性方向低分诊，两个模型接近性别平衡，另一个模型敏感性高但男性方向不对称较弱。DeepSeek 虽有明显方向性偏差，却具有较低的与入院结局相关的校准差距。人口学遮蔽显著降低 Gemini 翻转率至 0.5%，但 DeepSeek 在保留年龄的遮蔽设定下仍有残余偏差。链式思维提示降低所有模型准确率。

Conclusion: LLM 分诊公平性不能仅依赖单一指标判断：群体平等、反事实不变性和性别校准是不同性质的公平目标。不同模型的偏差来源不同，干预策略效果也不同，因此临床部署前必须进行逐模型、反事实层面的公平性审计。

Abstract: Emergency department triage assigns patients an acuity score that determines treatment priority, and clinical evidence documents persistent gender disparities in human acuity assessment. As hospitals pilot large language models (LLMs) as triage decision support, a critical question is whether these models reproduce or mitigate known biases. We present EQUITRIAGE, a fairness audit of LLM-based ESI assignment evaluating five models (Gemini-3-Flash, Nemotron-3-Super, DeepSeek-V3.1, Mistral-Small-3.2, GPT-4.1-Nano) across 374,275 evaluations on 18,714 MIMIC-IV-ED vignettes under four prompt strategies. Of 9,368 originals, 9,346 are paired with a gender-swapped counterfactual. All five models produced flip rates above a pre-registered 5% threshold (9.9% to 43.8%). Two showed directional female undertriage (DeepSeek F/M 2.15:1, Gemini 1.34:1); two were near-parity; one had high sensitivity with weak male-direction asymmetry. DeepSeek's directional bias coexisted with a low outcome-linked calibration gap (0.013 against MIMIC-IV admission), a Chouldechova-style dissociation between within-group calibration and between-pair counterfactual invariance. Demographic blinding reduced Gemini's flip rate to 0.5%; an age-preserving blind variant left DeepSeek with residual F/M 1.25, implicating age as a residual channel. Chain-of-thought prompting degraded accuracy for all five models. A two-model ablation reveals opposite underlying mechanisms for the same directional phenotype: in Gemini the signal is emergent in the combined name+gender swap, while in DeepSeek the gender token alone carries it. EQUITRIAGE shows that group parity, counterfactual invariance, and gender calibration are distinct fairness properties, that intervention effectiveness is model-dependent, and that per-model counterfactual auditing should precede clinical deployment.

</details>


### [104] [Rethinking Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval: Evaluating and Advancing Retrievers in Agentic Search Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04018)
*Yilun Zhao,Jinbiao Wei,Tingyu Song,Siyue Zhang,Chen Zhao,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 BRIGHT-Pro 基准与 RTriever-Synth 训练语料，用于更好评估和训练面向复杂推理的检索器；并微调得到 RTriever-4B，在多类检索器对比中显著优于基座模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理密集型检索需要返回可支撑下游推理的互补证据，而不仅是主题相似文本。现有评测基准金标准证据范围较窄、常孤立评估检索器；合成训练语料也多关注单段落相关性，难以训练证据组合能力。

Method: 作者构建专家标注基准 BRIGHT-Pro，为每个查询扩展多方面 gold evidence，并在静态检索与智能体式迭代搜索协议下评估检索器。同时构建 RTriever-Synth：基于方面分解生成互补正例与以正例为条件的困难负例，并用其对源自 Qwen3-Embedding-4B 的 RTriever-4B 进行 LoRA 微调。

Result: 实验覆盖词法检索器、通用检索器和推理密集型检索器。结果显示，方面感知评测与智能体式评测能够揭示标准指标难以观察到的检索行为；RTriever-4B 相比其基座模型取得大幅提升。

Conclusion: 论文强调推理密集型检索应从单一相关性匹配转向多方面、互补证据组合能力的评估与训练。BRIGHT-Pro 和 RTriever-Synth 为该方向提供了更合适的基准与训练资源，RTriever-4B 证明了方面分解式合成数据对检索器微调的有效性。

Abstract: Reasoning-intensive retrieval aims to surface evidence that supports downstream reasoning rather than merely matching topical similarity. This capability is increasingly important for agentic search systems, where retrievers must provide complementary evidence across iterative search and synthesis. However, existing work remains limited on both evaluation and training: benchmarks such as BRIGHT provide narrow gold sets and evaluate retrievers in isolation, while synthetic training corpora often optimize single-passage relevance rather than evidence portfolio construction. We introduce BRIGHT-Pro, an expert-annotated benchmark that expands each query with multi-aspect gold evidence and evaluates retrievers under both static and agentic search protocols. We further construct RTriever-Synth, an aspect-decomposed synthetic corpus that generates complementary positives and positive-conditioned hard negatives, and use it to LoRA fine-tune RTriever-4B from Qwen3-Embedding-4B. Experiments across lexical, general-purpose, and reasoning-intensive retrievers show that aspect-aware and agentic evaluation expose behaviors hidden by standard metrics, while RTriever-4B substantially improves over its base model.

</details>


### [105] [Safety and accuracy follow different scaling laws in clinical large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04039)
*Sebastian Wind,Tri-Thien Nguyen,Jeta Sopa,Mahshad Lotfinia,Sebastian Bickelhaup,Michael Uder,Harald Köstler,Gerhard Wellein,Sven Nebelung,Daniel Truhn,Andreas Maier,Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 SaFE-Scale 临床大模型安全评估框架，并构建 RadSaFE-200 放射学安全基准，发现安全性并不会随模型规模、上下文长度或推理算力自动提升，关键取决于证据质量、检索设计与部署方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学场景中，平均准确率不足以代表安全性；少量高置信度、高风险或与证据矛盾的错误可能造成严重后果。现有临床 LLM 扩展通常默认更大模型、更长上下文、更复杂检索或更多推理计算会带来更安全行为，但该假设缺乏系统验证。

Method: 作者提出 SaFE-Scale 框架，从模型规模、证据质量、检索策略、上下文暴露和推理时计算等维度评估临床 LLM 安全性；同时构建 RadSaFE-200 基准，包含 200 道放射学多选题，并提供干净证据、冲突证据以及选项级高风险错误、不安全答案和证据矛盾标签。实验评估 34 个本地部署 LLM，覆盖闭卷零样本、干净证据、冲突证据、标准 RAG、智能体式 RAG 和最大上下文提示六种部署条件。

Result: 干净证据带来最显著收益：平均准确率从 73.5% 提升到 94.1%，高风险错误从 12.0% 降至 2.6%，证据矛盾从 12.7% 降至 2.3%，危险过度自信从 8.0% 降至 1.6%。标准 RAG 与智能体式 RAG 未能复现该安全表现；智能体式 RAG 相比标准 RAG 提高准确率并降低矛盾率，但高风险错误和危险过度自信仍偏高。最大上下文提示增加延迟但未弥合安全差距，额外推理时计算仅带来有限收益。最坏情况分析显示，临床重要错误集中在少量问题上。

Conclusion: 临床 LLM 安全性不是模型扩展的被动结果，而是由证据质量、检索设计、上下文构造和群体失败模式共同决定的部署属性。相比单纯追求更大模型或更长上下文，临床部署应优先优化可靠证据供给、检索质量控制和针对高风险失败模式的安全评估。

Abstract: Clinical LLMs are often scaled by increasing model size, context length, retrieval complexity, or inference-time compute, with the implicit expectation that higher accuracy implies safer behavior. This assumption is incomplete in medicine, where a few confident, high-risk, or evidence-contradicting errors can matter more than average benchmark performance. We introduce SaFE-Scale, a framework for measuring how clinical LLM safety changes across model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute. To instantiate this framework, we introduce RadSaFE-200, a Radiology Safety-Focused Evaluation benchmark of 200 multiple-choice questions with clinician-defined clean evidence, conflict evidence, and option-level labels for high-risk error, unsafe answer, and evidence contradiction. We evaluated 34 locally deployed LLMs across six deployment conditions: closed-book prompting (zero-shot), clean evidence, conflict evidence, standard RAG, agentic RAG, and max-context prompting. Clean evidence produced the strongest improvement, increasing mean accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1%, while reducing high-risk error from 12.0% to 2.6%, contradiction from 12.7% to 2.3%, and dangerous overconfidence from 8.0% to 1.6%. Standard RAG and agentic RAG did not reproduce this safety profile: agentic RAG improved accuracy over standard RAG and reduced contradiction, but high-risk error and dangerous overconfidence remained elevated. Max-context prompting increased latency without closing the safety gap, and additional inference-time compute produced only limited gains. Worst-case analysis showed that clinically consequential errors concentrated in a small subset of questions. Clinical LLM safety is therefore not a passive consequence of scaling, but a deployment property shaped by evidence quality, retrieval design, context construction, and collective failure behavior.

</details>
